# Continuation Prompt ‚Äî TI-84 Plus CE ROM Transpilation

> ‚öÝ **Auto-continuation loop active** ‚Äî Windows Task Scheduler `TI84-AutoContinuation` fires a headless Opus session every 1h (daily trigger at midnight, then hourly repeat). Before editing this file in a human session, check `git log --oneline` for recent `auto-session N` commits and consider `schtasks /change /tn "TI84-AutoContinuation" /disable` to prevent conflicts. Re-enable with `/enable`. Change interval: `schtasks /change /tn "TI84-AutoContinuation" /ri <minutes>`. Launcher: `scripts/auto-continuation.bat`. Logs: `logs/auto-session-*.log` (gitignored).

**Last updated**: 2026-04-30 (session 164 ‚Äî Phase 25CQ: 3 sub-priorities completed. **KEY FINDINGS**: (1) **0x068B78 FULLY DECODED** ‚Äî P1 disassembled 12 instructions (0x068B78-0x068B9F). TWO entry points: 0x068B78 (gcd path) = CALL 0x07FA74 (ConstLoader) + JP 0x07F831 (TypeValidator) ‚Äî just loads OP2=1.0 then tail-calls TypeValidator. 0x068B80 (alternate, not used by gcd) = more elaborate validator with ExponentCheck, CP 0x84 bound, etc. Both gcd calls (step 17 and 736) take identical 15-block path. Exit: Z=false, C=false, A=exponent-0x80 (A=1 for OP1=12, A=2 for OP1=100). OP2 always replaced with 1.0 regardless of entry value. (2) **OUTER LOOP PATH FULLY TRACED (steps 332-735)** ‚Äî P2 dense trace of all 410 steps. Flow: 0x068DA3‚Üígcd_LoadType(A=0x50)‚ÜíSetxxxxOP2(100, builds OP2=100 via multiplication loop)‚ÜíFPAdd(OP1+OP2, with OP1=0)‚ÜíPushRealO1‚ÜíOP4ToOP1(OP4=1200‚ÜíOP1)‚ÜíFDiv100(OP1/100)‚ÜíOP1toOP2+normalize‚ÜíInvSub‚ÜíJmpThru‚ÜíOP1ToOP6‚Üígcd_helper‚ÜíOP5‚ÜíOP2‚Üísecond InvSub‚Üísecond JmpThru‚ÜíPOP AF/CALL Z path at 0x061D0E/0x03E1xx‚Üíreturns to 0x068D45‚ÜíPushRealO1‚ÜíPopRealO1‚Üífalls through to 0x068D4D‚Üí0x068D61 (LOOP RE-ENTRY). **RE-ENTRY IS VIA FALL-THROUGH from 0x068D4D to 0x068D61**, NOT a jump back to 0x068D5D. (3) **OP2=12 AT STEP 535 COMES FROM OP1‚ÜíOP2 COPY** ‚Äî P3 traced every OP2 mutation steps 330-540. At step 447, OP1‚ÜíOP2 copy (0x07F8FA) fires: OP1=[00 81 12...]=12 copied into OP2 (was 100). OP1 retained original value 12 throughout the division computation. NOT from FPS pop (only 1 FPS change: PUSH at step 427). NOT from OP4/OP5. The OP1‚ÜíOP2 copy is part of the compound function at 0x07C747 in the outer-loop processing. Seeds: 50,058. Blocks: 143,616. Covered: 699,830 (95.93%). Codex: not dispatched (stalled since session 96). Sonnet: 3/3 completed and verified by Opus. Golden regression 26/26 PASS.)

---

## ‚òÖ Strategic Reframing (READ FIRST)

**The 16.65% "plateau" is a denominator artifact**, not a reachability problem. ROM is 4 MB but **82.6% (3,464,815 bytes) is erased flash (0xFF fill)** ‚Äî fundamentally uncoverable. The genuine executable+data ROM is **729,489 non-erased bytes**, and the transpiler already covers **95.92% of them**.

Of the remaining ~30 KB of uncovered non-erased bytes:

| Verdict | Bytes | % |
|---------|-------|---|
| CODE? (decodable) | ~13 KB | 29% |
| DATA-MIXED | ~24 KB | 52% |
| DATA-SPARSE | ~6 KB | 13% |
| STRINGS | ~3 KB | 6% |

Only ~13 KB is plausibly executable code, scattered across ~3,400 tiny ranges (top hole = 62 bytes). **Coverage work is effectively done.** Future sessions should pivot to feature work. Use `audit-true-uncovered.mjs` for true coverage, not `coveragePercent`.

---

## Current State

- **True coverage**: 95.93% (699,830 / 729,489 non-erased bytes)
- **Reported coverage**: 16.69% (143,616 blocks)
- **Seed count**: 50,058
- **Live stubs**: 0. **OS jump table**: 980/980. **ISR dispatch gate**: unlocked.
- **Keyboard scan, ISR dispatch, VRAM pipeline, OS init, real boot, home-screen render**: all working end-to-end.
- **Golden regression** (`node TI-84_Plus_CE/probe-phase99d-home-verify.mjs`): 26/26 exact at row 39 col 2, "Normal Float Radian" 3/3 PASS, status dots PASS (36 fg pixels), total 1004 fg pixels.
- `ROM.transpiled.js` gitignored (~214 MB). `.gz` committed (~16 MB, regenerate with `gzip -k -9 ROM.transpiled.js`).
- **Per-stage IX convention**: home-screen stages 1‚Äì4 all need `IX = 0xD1A860` before entry. Stage 3 exit IX = `0xe00800`, others = `0x0159bd`. Don't use `IX = SP` (crashes stages 1/4 at 0x58c35b).
- **Display buffer 0xD006C0 has no natural OS populator**. Browser-shell seeds it via restore path 0x088720 (seed 260 bytes into backup buffer 0xD02EC7, then call 0x088720).

## Next-Session Priorities

> **Status update (2026-04-30, session 163)**: Session 163 completed 3 sub-priorities. **KEY FINDINGS**: (1) **LOOP TOP DOES NOT RESTORE OP2** ‚Äî 0x068D5D-0x068D81 contains no OP register copies. CALL 0x068B78 is a type validator that sets OP2=1.0. Exponent bounds check (0x82-0x84). Falls into body. (2) **OUTER LOOP STRUCTURE DECODED** ‚Äî Steps 333-734 are post-inner-loop processing. JR NZ at step 332 does NOT go to 0x068D5D ‚Äî execution continues at 0x068DA3. Loop top re-entry only at step 735 for iteration 2. OP5‚ÜíOP2 at step 570 is in the OUTER region. (3) **OP4 PRE-LOADING DISPROVEN** ‚Äî OP4=8.0 and OP4=800 both still produce E_Domain. The OP4‚ÜíOP2 copy is intentional (restores saved OP1 for InvSub), but the bug is that BOTH InvSub operands end up being OP1 because the compound OP1‚ÜíOP2 call at 0x07C747 destroys the divisor.

### 1. ‚òÖ‚òÖ‚òÖ FP gcd ‚Äî Trace the COMPLETE two-iteration algorithm to find the root cause
Session 164 answered all 4 critical questions from session 163. The algorithm is now fully mapped: (a) 0x068B78 = ConstLoader(1.0) + TypeValidator tail-call. (b) Outer-loop path: post-inner-loop at 0x068DA3 does gcd_LoadType‚ÜíSetxxxxOP2(100)‚ÜíFPAdd‚ÜíPushRealO1‚ÜíOP4ToOP1‚ÜíFDiv100‚ÜíOP1toOP2+normalize‚ÜíInvSub‚ÜíJmpThru‚ÜíOP1ToOP6‚Üígcd_helper‚ÜíOP5‚ÜíOP2‚ÜíInvSub‚ÜíJmpThru‚ÜíPOP AF path‚Üíreturns to 0x068D45‚Üífalls through to 0x068D61 (loop re-entry). (c) OP2=12 at InvSub comes from OP1‚ÜíOP2 copy at 0x07F8FA ‚Äî OP1 retains original value 12 throughout. (d) Re-entry is fall-through from 0x068D4D‚Üí0x068D61, not a jump.
**ROOT CAUSE STILL UNKNOWN.** The algorithm computes InvSub(OP1, OP1) = 0 in the inner loop (because OP4=OP1, so OP4‚ÜíOP2 restores OP1 into OP2, making both InvSub operands equal). This produces mod=0 instead of mod=4 for gcd(12,8). The DIVISOR (8) is lost during the compound OP1‚ÜíOP2 call at 0x07C747.
**NEXT STEPS**: (a) **Compare with a WORKING gcd input** ‚Äî find a pair (a,b) where gcd succeeds (if any). Try gcd(4,2), gcd(6,3), gcd(10,5) ‚Äî pairs where one divides the other evenly. If ALL fail, the issue is systemic in our transpilation. (b) **Trace the compound function 0x07C747 with DIFFERENT OP1‚âÝOP2** ‚Äî session 160 showed OP1==OP2 at entry. Is 0x07C747 supposed to receive OP1‚âÝOP2 (i.e., is the OP1‚ÜíOP2 copy at 0x07F8FA BEFORE 0x07C747 wrong)? Check the ROM bytes at 0x068D82 to confirm the call sequence. (c) **Focus on the inner body call sequence** at 0x068D82: the order is OP1‚ÜíOP4, CALL 0x07C747 (compound OP1‚ÜíOP2), OP1‚ÜíOP3, OP4‚ÜíOP2, InvSub. What if the compound call is supposed to compute something other than OP1‚ÜíOP2? Session 161 showed it's a NO-OP for OP1 (normalizes to 0, adds OP2, copies back). Maybe the REAL purpose is the side effect on OP2 (normalization), not the OP1‚ÜíOP2 copy.
Key probes: `probe-phase164-068b78-disasm.mjs` (P1), `probe-phase164-outer-loop-trace.mjs` (P2), `probe-phase164-op2-source-trace.mjs` (P3).

### Completed (session 160)
- ‚úÖ **Phase 25CM ‚Äî OP1TOOP2 COMPOUND FUNCTION DECODED + NORMALIZATION CONFIRMED CORRECT + ALL EXP>=0x80 INPUTS DESTROYED (3 SUB-PRIORITIES, 1 MAJOR ARCHITECTURAL INSIGHT)**: **(P1) ROM disassembly of 0x07C74B + 0x07CA48 + caller scan**: Built `probe-phase160-07c74b-disasm.mjs`. Final FPS=0xD1AA12 > initial 0xD1AA00 = stack leak. **ROOT CAUSE**: gcd handler's const 1.0 loader is intentional but the FPS pop that should restore OP2=8.0 before division is missing or too late. NEXT: disassemble 0x068D41-0x068B7C to find the missing pop path; test manual OP2 restore at step 20. Sonnet: 3/3 completed and verified by Opus. Golden regression 26/26 PASS. - ‚úÖ **Phase 25CE ‚Äî IPOINT 16BPP COLOR MECHANISM FULLY DECODED + 4/4 COLOR TESTS PASS (P2, CLOSES INVESTIGATION + CORRECTS SESSION 151)**: Built `probe-phase152-ipoint-color-fix.mjs`. **Part A (disassembly 0x07B5B6‚Üí0x07B682)**: Block 0x07B5B6 = `BIT 7,(IY+30); JR NZ,0x07B62B` ‚Äî conditional jump to color-decision block. Block 0x07B62B = `PUSH AF; POP AF; OR A; LD DE,(mbase<<16|0x26AC); JR NZ,0x07B677` ‚Äî loads drawFGColor (16-bit) into DE, uses A (drawMode) only as boolean (NZ = draw, Z = erase). Block 0x07B677 = `LD BC,(0xD02A8A)` ‚Äî loads VRAM pointer. Block 0x07B682 = **`LD A,E; LD (BC),A`** ‚Äî writes drawFGColor LOW byte (NOT drawMode as session 151 claimed). `LD A,E` REPLACES drawMode in A with drawFGColor_lo. Block 0x07B68A = `INC BC; LD A,D; LD (BC),A` ‚Äî writes drawFGColor HIGH byte. **Session 151's claim "first pixel byte = drawMode" was WRONG** ‚Äî A=0x01 at block entry gets replaced by `LD A,E` before the store. Session 151 saw VRAM=0x01 because drawFGColor was 0x0000 (E=0x00 ‚Üí stored 0x00, not the A=0x01 drawMode). **Part B (4-color test)**: Blue (drawFGColor=0x001F): VRAM=[0x1F, 0x00] ‚úì. Red (0xF800): VRAM=[0x00, 0xF8] ‚úì. Green (0x07E0): VRAM=[0xE0, 0x07] ‚úì. White (0xFFFF): VRAM=[0xFF, 0xFF] ‚úì. All match drawFGColor in little-endian BGR565. **Part C (encoding analysis)**: 16bpp pixel = drawFGColor stored LE as [E=fgLo, D=fgHi]. Only 2 bytes per pixel (bytes 3-4 remain sentinel). drawMode is used purely as a boolean gate (NZ‚Üídraw, Z‚Üíerase). drawColorCode (0xD026AE) is used only by 8bpp plotSScreen Z-path, not the 16bpp LCD VRAM NZ-path. VRAM address uses inverted Y: (0xEF-C)√ó0xA0√ó2, not naive Y√ó640. **IPOINT COLOR INVESTIGATION IS CLOSED.** For colored graph pixels: seed drawFGColor at 0xD026AC with BGR565 value before IPoint call. Sonnet P2: completed and verified by Opus. Codex P2: stalled (0 bytes). Golden regression 26/26 PASS.

Test 1: ILine (5,5)‚Üí(50,50) = 26 non-zero bytes (safe range X<64). Test 2: ILine box (4 sides) = **147 non-zero bytes** ‚Äî multiple ILine calls accumulate correctly in plotSScreen. Test 3: GraphPars (0x09986C) stalls at step 84 ‚Äî **missing block 0x0998CA** (contains `RES 3,(IY+0x48)`, `RES 5,(IY+0x14)`, `AND 0x7F`, `CP 0x08`). BCD graph window correctly seeded (Xmin=-10, Xmax=10, Ymin=-10, Ymax=10). Test 4: DrawCmd (0x05DD96) **returns successfully** in 79,764 steps but 0 pixels ‚Äî correctly finds no Y-equations. Hot loop at 0x09EFDE (11,684 hits), draw loop at 0x06F2E2-0x06F341 (~21K hits). Next: seed 0x0998CA + Y-equation data. Sonnet P2. Golden regression 26/26 PASS.
- ‚úÖ **Phase 25BJ ‚Äî BUFINSERT CALLING CONVENTION CORRECTED (P3, MAJOR FIX)**: Built `probe-phase131-edit-buffer-disasm.mjs`. **CRITICAL DISCOVERY**: BufInsert (0x05E2A0) takes token in **DE** register (E=token byte, D=two-byte flag), NOT BC as sessions 129-130 assumed. First instruction is `PUSH DE`, then `CALL room-check` (0x05E3D6), then `POP BC` ‚Äî this POP overwrites BC with the saved DE value. Prior sessions passed token in BC, which was clobbered by POP ‚Üí garbage bytes (pointer metadata from whatever was in DE) and +2 stride (non-zero D triggered two-byte path). **With correct convention (E=token, D=0)**: cursor advances +1 per token, buffer stores raw token bytes `32 70 33` = "2+3", 7 steps per insertion. Room-check at 0x05E3D6 loads editCursor (0xD0243A) and editTail (0xD0243D), compares via SBC at 0x0CC973. CreateNumEditBuf (0x096E09) confirmed NOT initializing pointers ‚Äî manual init works. Key-to-token conversion uses cascading CP/JP dispatch at 0x045C37 (not single indexed table); digit keys k0-k9 (0x8E-0x97) likely convert via `token = kCode - 0x8E + 0x30`. Sonnet P3. Golden regression 26/26 PASS.
- Golden regression 26/26 PASS (bestMatch=row39 col2, Normal/Float/Radian 3/3, status dots PASS). Codex: not dispatched (stalling since session 96). Sonnet: 3/3 completed and verified by Opus.

### Completed (session 129)
- ‚úÖ **Phase 25BH ‚Äî FP DISPATCH TABLE FULLY MAPPED (P1)**: Built `probe-phase129-fp-dispatch.mjs`. Dispatch chain at 0x0686EF (not 0x0686D3 ‚Äî that's a data region) is a CP/JR Z chain with 16 handled operation codes: 0x08, 0x1C, 0x20, 0x21, 0x80, 0x88, 0x89, 0x8C, 0x90, 0x98, 0x99, 0x9C, 0xC8, 0xC9, 0xCC, 0xD0. **0xDA (min) and 0xDB (max) NOT in table** ‚Äî fall through all 16 comparisons to catch-all `JP 0x06677B` ‚Üí JError ‚Üí LCD busy-wait. **gcd(12,8) with op code 0xD5 SUCCEEDS** ‚Äî returns via FAKE_RET in 3386 steps, but OP1=0.588003 (wrong result, expected 4). Missing block at 0x06859B likely responsible. **KEY FINDING**: At dispatch entry (0x0686EF), A=0x00 for ALL three functions ‚Äî the dispatch is NOT comparing the raw op code. The actual op code (0xDA/0xDB/0xD5) sits on OPS. The upstream dispatcher reads OPS and derives A before reaching this table. LCD mem-patching (RET at 0x001221) ineffective ‚Äî transpiled blocks execute pre-compiled JS, not memory bytes. Sonnet P1.
- ‚úÖ **Phase 25BH ‚Äî IPoint WORKS: PIXELS WRITTEN TO plotSScreen (P2, MAJOR MILESTONE)**: Built `probe-phase129-graph-render.mjs` with 5 scenarios. **drawMode=1 (normal draw) at coordinates (10,10) ‚Üí 1 pixel written to plotSScreen[0x1B8E]=0xF0 in 47 steps. drawMode=2 (XOR) also writes pixels (53 steps).** Root causes of prior failures identified: (a) drawMode=0 = ERASE (OS DECrements A internally; A=0‚ÜíDEC‚Üí0xFF‚Üíerase path writes color 0x00 = invisible on empty buffer). Correct draw mode is A=1. (b) Bounds-check at 0x07B793 requires seeded pixWideP (0xD014FE, 16-bit width) and pixWide_m_2 (0xD01501, 16-bit height) ‚Äî with zeros, ALL coordinates fail. X bounds use 8-bit `CP L` comparison ‚Äî coordinates ‚â• low byte of pixWideP fail (e.g., with pixWideP=320, L=0x40, so X‚â•64 fails). MBASE confirmed 0xD0 at bounds-check in all scenarios. RAM seeding map: 0xD014FE=width, 0xD01501=height, 0xD026AE=pen color (2 bytes), 0xD000B5 bit 7=0 (hookflags3). Pixel write mechanism at 0x07B7CC: loads pen color from 0xD02A60, computes plotSScreen offset, writes nibble. Sonnet P2.
- ‚úÖ **Phase 25BH ‚Äî EDIT BUFFER SYSTEM FULLY MAPPED (P3, RESEARCH)**: Built `probe-phase129-edit-buffer.mjs`. **Edit buffer = gap buffer**: editTop=0xD02437, editCursor=0xD0243A, editTail=0xD0243D, editBtm=0xD02440 (all 24-bit pointers). editSym=0xD0244E, editDat=0xD02451. **OS routines resolved**: BufClr‚Üí0x0ADAC3 (returned 351 steps but didn't init pointers ‚Äî needs pre-initialized buffer), BufInsert‚Üí0x05E2A0 (token in C/BC, calls 0x05E3D6 room check, updates editCursor at 0xD0243A), BufDelete‚Üí0x05E367, BufLeft‚Üí0x05E242, BufRight‚Üí0x05E27E, CreateNumEditBuf‚Üí0x096E09 (likely the actual initializer). **Key codes corrected**: k0=0x8E through k9=0x97 (NOT scan codes). ## Research-Informed Refinements (added 2026-04-24 from external deep-research pass)

Grounded in TI-83 Plus SDK prose (parser/error-handler contracts), WikiTI 83+ memory-layout page, and the CE include mirror (ti84pceg.inc). Public record has **zero labels** for 0x099211 / 0x099910 / 0x07FF81 / 0x08BF22 / 0x0831A4 / 0x09215E / 0x04C940 ‚Äî our RE is the source of truth on those. Highlights that inform current priorities:

### R1. ‚úÖ RESOLVED (session 110) ‚Äî `pTempCnt` audit
pTempCnt at 0xD02596 is correctly zeroed by MEM_INIT (confirmed 0x000000). Stays zero throughout MEM_INIT ‚Üí CreateReal ‚Üí ParseInp pipeline and across all expression evaluations. NOT a factor in the RclVarSym failure.

### R2. ‚úÖ RESOLVED (session 111) ‚Äî Parser flags fully enumerated
Report flags these publicly-named knobs as likely ParseInp-sensitive (all from CE include):
- `ParsFlag`, `ParsFlag2` (including `numOP1` = "result in OP1")
- `onFlags.parseInput`
- `fmtFlags`, `numMode`, `fmtOverride`
- `graphFlags2.splitOverride`
- `newDispF.allowProgTokens`, `progExecuting`
- `hookflags4.parserHookActive` + `parserHookPtr`

**Action**: enumerate each against postInitState. Current probes may accidentally inherit a clean zero-state that works, but any leftover bit from a prior CoorMon iteration would silently change ParseInp's branch. Deterministic seed = deterministic trace.

### R3. ‚úÖ RESOLVED (session 110) ‚Äî Descending-boundary invariant
Invariant holds after MEM_INIT and after CreateReal, but **VIOLATED after ParseInp** in ALL cases:
- `FPSbase > FPS` (FPS underflows 9 bytes below base ‚Äî one 9-byte FP value pushed downward)
- `OPS > OPBase` (OPS overflows 6-12 bytes above base ‚Äî operator stack grows upward past boundary)
This is the root cause of VAT entry corruption (priority 1). ParseInp does not clean up FPS/OPS after evaluation ‚Äî the OS normally handles this between stages.

### R4. ‚úÖ RESOLVED (session 110) ‚Äî 0x099211 is NOT ParseInpGraph
Static disassembly of 300 bytes confirms: 0x099211 is a "DisarmScroll" / variable-recall-to-edit-buffer routine. No CALL/JP to ParseInp (0x099914), no trampoline reference (0x099910), no PushErrorHandler (0x061DEF), and ZERO IY ops in the ParsFlag area (IY+0x44 through IY+0x4C). All 8 IY operations target lower offsets (statFlags at IY+0x09, IY+0x01, IY+0x05). Session 98's "DisarmScroll" name was correct. The ParseInpGraph hypothesis is disproved for this address.

### R5. ‚òÖ Treat `errSP` as RAM snapshot, not live SP (mental model fix)
TI's 83+ `ResetStacks` comment is explicit: `(onsp)‚Üí(errsp), (fpbase)‚Üí(fps), (opbase)‚Üí(ops)`. `errSP` is a RAM-saved snapshot distinct from the hardware SP. Our session-108 18-byte frame-pop finding is reverse-engineered behavior (TI only publishes "six pushes" + SP/FPS/OPS restore), so brittle by design. Implication: when diagnosing trampoline/SP-shift issues, track `errSP` (RAM) and `SP` (CPU) as **two independent state variables** and log both in error-path probes.

### Completed (session 113)
- ‚úÖ **Phase 25BB ‚Äî DIRECT-EVAL TOKEN MAPPING EXTENDED (P1)**: Extended `EVAL_TOKEN_MAP` with 50+ new entries: scientific notation E (0x3B), power ^ (0x0F), comma (0x2B), œÄ (0xAC), A-Z uppercase (0x41-0x5A), a-z lowercase (same tokens, 'e' unmapped). Added multi-character token matching: Ans, sin, cos, tan, ln, log, sqrt, abs, e^, plus ‚àö unicode. Added whitespace skipping. Updated negation context for comma, ^, and function tokens. Codex P1 did bulk mapping; Sonnet P1 added negation triggers. Golden regression 26/26 PASS.
- ‚úÖ **Phase 25BB ‚Äî RCLVARSYM APPROACH B BOUNDARY CHECK ROOT CAUSE (P2)**: Built `probe-phase25bb-rclvarsym-disasm.mjs` with block-by-block trace comparison. **EXACT DIVERGENCE**: Step 8 at PC=0x084716 ‚Äî FindSym compares DE against HL=0xD3FFF9 (stale boundary from default OPBase). Scenario A: DE=0xD3FFEE < limit ‚Üí found. Scenario B: DE=0xD4004F > limit ‚Üí carry ‚Üí error path ‚Üí copies from HL=0xFFFFAA ‚Üí garbage OP1. NOT an off-by-N error ‚Äî it's a stale boundary limit never updated for non-default OPBase. Approach B definitively closed. Sonnet P2.
- Golden regression 26/26 PASS. Codex: P1 completed (token mapping). Sonnet: P1 completed (negation triggers), P2 completed (RclVarSym trace).

- ‚úÖ **Phase 25AW ‚Äî TRAMPOLINE INVESTIGATION COMPLETE (KEY SYNTHESIS)**: Sessions 99-108 fully characterized the trampoline path (0x0586E3‚Üí0x099910‚Üí0x07FF81‚ÜíParseInp). Root cause of trampoline failure: accidental error frame stack alignment. The trampoline's extra CALL shifts all stack positions by 3 bytes, moving 0x099929 from the HL (catch address) position to the AF (flags) position in JError's 18-byte frame pop. Fix: errSP must be set to ParseInp_SP - 6 (dynamic, not fixed). But the trampoline adds nothing for expression evaluation ‚Äî 0x07FF81's List pre-seed is overwritten by ParseInp (session 100). **Direct ParseInp at 0x099914 with OP1=zeros is the correct and fully working approach.** Close the trampoline investigation; focus on full ENTER-handler simulation with direct ParseInp.

- ‚úÖ **Phase 25AT ‚Äî STACK DEPTH MISMATCH = ROOT CAUSE OF VIA-CALL FAILURE (KEY FINDING)**: With corrected validated-scratch seeding (tokens at 0xD00800, endPC=0xD00803), direct ParseInp at 0x099914 returns OP1=5.0, errNo=0x8D in 918 steps (matches baseline exactly). This 3-byte SP difference causes ParseInp's internal routines to trigger compaction. The trampoline 0x07FF81 is benign (just sets OP1 type/index, same as baseline). Fix: increase mainSP by 3-6 bytes to compensate for the extra call depth.
- ‚úÖ **Phase 25AT ‚Äî NZ-PATH RE-SEED APPROACH IS A DEAD END (NEGATIVE RESULT)**: Re-seed probe ran ENTER handler at 0x0585E9 with forced NZ (bit 5 of 0xD000C4 set), 200K step budget, step-by-step with OPBase watchpoint. Three re-seeds fired (step 244: InsertMem adjustment, step 362: LDDR compaction at 0x083214, step 1920: RAM CLEAR at 0x001881). But POP AF at 0x05862F was NEVER reached ‚Äî the early call chain (0x07FF7B at step 44, 0x08384F at step 50) runs before the NZ/Z branch and triggers RAM CLEAR ‚Üí HALT loop at 0x006202 (197,932 of 200K hits). The NZ path requires far more OS state than just allocator pointers. **Implication: the bypass approach (entering at 0x0586CE) is definitively the correct strategy.**

- ‚úÖ **Phase 25AS ‚Äî COMMON TAIL FULLY DISASSEMBLED + 0x09215E = SOLE BLOCKER (KEY FINDING)**: Static disassembly of 0x058693-0x058700 (common tail), 0x082961, and 0x09215E. Common tail has 13 CALLs before ParseInp at 0x0586E3. **0x082961 is NOT a blocker**: it's a simple FPS push ‚Äî `LD HL,0xD005F8` (OP1), pushes 9 bytes onto FP stack at (FPS), updates FPS pointer at 0xD0258D. Completes in 12 steps. **0x09215E IS the blocker**: calls 0x0800B8 (BIT 5,(IY+0x44)), takes JR Z to 0x092177 (bit 5 is 0 after MEM_INIT), which chains through FindSym region to 0x0BD19F ‚Üí LCD display infinite loop (0x0BD19F‚Üí0x05E386‚Üí0x0A2A45‚Üí0x0A2B51‚Üí0x0A2A49‚Üírepeat, consuming all 10K budget). **JR NZ at 0x0586CC confirmed NOT taken**: bit 4 of (IY+52) = mem[0xD000B4] = 0x00 after MEM_INIT, so the branch that would skip ParseInp is NOT active. **Recommendation: enter at 0x0586CE** (past 0x09215E and the BIT 4 test) to bypass the LCD loop and reach ParseInp. Fallback: 0x0586E3 (direct CALL 0x099910). Sonnet P2. Artifacts: `probe-phase25as-common-tail-disasm.mjs`, `phase25as-common-tail-disasm-report.md`.

### Completed (session 103)
- ‚úÖ **Phase 25AR ‚Äî ALLOCATOR POINTER ADDRESSES CORRECTED FROM ti84pceg.inc (MAJOR CORRECTION)**: Session 102's priority text used WRONG addresses for pTemp (0xD02593) and progPtr (0xD0259C). Correct addresses from ti84pceg.inc: OPBase=0xD02590, OPS=0xD02593, pTempCnt=0xD02596 (4 bytes), pTemp=0xD0259A, progPtr=0xD0259D. 0xD02593 is actually OPS (parser expression stack), NOT pTemp. Session 82's MEM_INIT disassembly correctly identified these (they were in the address map at line 369-373 all along), but the priority text propagated wrong addresses. FindSym at 0x083865 reads pTemp from 0xD0259A and progPtr from 0xD0259D for its VAT scan loop exit condition (`SBC HL,DE` where DE=pTemp+1). Correcting these addresses fixed the FindSym infinite loop.
- ‚úÖ **Phase 25AR ‚Äî EMPTY-ENTER PATH CANNOT REACH PARSEINP (STATIC PROOF)**: Disassembly of 0x058630-0x058695. The branch at 0x058637 (`JP Z, 0x058C65`) is a JP not a CALL ‚Äî no return address pushed. When 0x058C65's RET executes, it pops the return address of whoever CALLed 0x0585E9 (CoorMon), not the instruction after the JP. The common tail at 0x058693 is only reachable via: (a) NZ path at 0x058630 `JR NZ 0x05866A` ‚Üí allocator calls ‚Üí falls through to 0x058693, or (b) history-recall path (numLastEntries>0) at 0x05863B-0x058668 ‚Üí `JR 0x058693`. Empty-ENTER (numLastEntries=0) is a ParseInp dead end. Sonnet P3. Artifacts: `probe-phase25ar-post-empty-enter-disasm.mjs`, `phase25ar-post-empty-enter-disasm-report.md`.
- ‚úÖ **Phase 25AR ‚Äî OPBase SEEDING WORKS: Old VAT walker loop ELIMINATED**: With OPBase=0xD3FFFF at 0xD02590, the VAT walker loop at 0x082745 was NOT entered in the corrected-pointer probes. OPBase seeding is confirmed effective. However, other infinite loops emerged (FindSym at 0x0838xx when pTemp/progPtr wrong, allocator at 0x082745 when pointers get zeroed by internal routines).
- ‚úÖ **Phase 25AR ‚Äî FINDSYM LOOP AT 0x083865 FULLY DISASSEMBLED**: Loop exit condition: `SBC HL,DE; JR C, 0x0838C8` where HL=progPtr (walk position) and DE=pTemp+1 (boundary). Loop scans VAT entries backward from progPtr, reading type bytes (AND 0x3F), comparing variable names against OP1 (0xD005F8). Exit at 0x0838C8 = `POP DE; RET` (symbol not found). With pTemp=progPtr=0xD3FFFF (seeded correctly), the first iteration has HL=0xD3FFF8 < DE=0xD40000 ‚Üí carry ‚Üí immediate exit. Utility at 0x04C91C = zero-extend BC to 24 bits via scrapMem (0xD02AD7). Sonnet investigation. Artifacts: `probe-phase25ar-findsym-loop-disasm.mjs`, `phase25ar-findsym-loop-disasm-report.md`.
- ‚úÖ **Phase 25AR ‚Äî ALLOCATOR POINTERS ZEROED DURING ENTER HANDLER (NEW BLOCKER)**: Even with all allocator pointers seeded at correct addresses (OPBase=0xD3FFFF, pTemp=0xD3FFFF, progPtr=0xD3FFFF), the ENTER handler's early call chain (0x058D54‚Üí0x058BA3‚Üí0x05840B‚Üí0x05E7D8 at steps 6-29) ZEROES all pointers before reaching the allocator loop. Post-run: OPBase=0, pTemp=0, progPtr=0, FPSbase changed to 0x01049E (ROM address = corruption). This is the same compaction/LDDR sweep seen in sessions 95-97 (0x05E3A2‚Üí0x05E836‚Üí0x0831A4). The pointer zeroing is the REAL blocker ‚Äî it destroys seeded state before it can be used.
- ‚úÖ **Phase 25AR ‚Äî numLastEntries=2 STRATEGY FAILS (BOTH ENTRIES CONSUMED)**: With numLastEntries=2 and two seeded history entries, the history manager at 0x0921CB consumed BOTH entries (2‚Üí0, not 2‚Üí1). The recall check at 0x058632 then sees numLastEntries=0. Meanwhile the early call chain zeroed all allocator pointers ‚Üí VAT walker loop at 0x082745 (22,716 hits). The history-recall path (JR 0x058693) was never reached.

ParseInp at 0x0586E3 never reached. The pre-ParseInp calls in the common tail (0x082961, 0x09215E, 0x082902, 0x0A1FD1, 0x0A27DD) require more OS state than just allocator pointer seeding. Also: 0x0586CC `JR NZ 0x0586F3` could skip ParseInp if bit 4 of (IY+52) is set.

### Completed (session 102)
- ‚úÖ **Phase 25AQ ‚Äî VAT WALKER LOOP EXIT CONDITION FOUND (KEY FINDING)**: Static disassembly of 0x082745-0x0827CA. Loop structure: reads 3-byte VAT entry pointer via LD C,(HL)/DEC HL/LD B,(HL)/DEC HL/LD A,(HL), stores to scrapMem via CALL 0x04C876, calls 0x0821B2 (range check), optionally adjusts pointer, advances by entry size, then: `POP AF / OR A / SBC HL,BC / LD BC,(0xD02590) / SBC HL,BC / RET C`. **OPBase at 0xD02590 is the sole exit condition.** When HL (current walk position) drops below OPBase, the loop returns. With OPBase=0 (uninitialized), the comparison HL < 0 is unreachable in 24-bit unsigned arithmetic ‚Üí infinite loop. Also found: 0xD02577 is loaded during the loop (unknown allocator boundary), 0x04C876 is just a scrapMem store (not a compare), sub at 0x08279E reads entry type byte (AND 0x3F) for variable-type dispatch. Per-pointer adjuster at 0x0827CA-0x082830 adjusts 11 system pointers if they fall within affected range. Sonnet P1. Artifacts: `probe-phase25aq-vat-walker-disasm.mjs`, `phase25aq-vat-walker-disasm-report.md`.
- ‚úÖ **Phase 25AQ ‚Äî HISTORY BUFFER SEED TESTED (CONFIRMS ALLOCATOR AS SOLE BLOCKER)**: Seeded minimal history entry: 2-byte LE size (0x0004) at 0xD0150B, 4 bytes token data "2+3\n" at 0xD0150D, end pointer 0xD01511 at 0xD01508. Set numLastEntries=1 at 0xD01D0B. ENTER handler at 0x0585E9 ran 100K steps. History manager at 0x0921CB reached at step 58, consumed the entry correctly (numLastEntries 1‚Üí0). But execution fell into allocator loop at 0x082754 instead of reaching 0x058693 (common tail). The allocator loop is the same OPBase=0 issue. **Implication**: once OPBase is seeded correctly, BOTH the empty-ENTER and history-recall paths should terminate and reach ParseInp. Also confirmed: the LDIR computation at 0x0922A2 is `BC = (0xD01508) - entryAddr`, confirming session 101's wraparound analysis. Sub-function 0x092FDD walks the buffer with `LD HL,0xD0150B; DEC A; RET Z` loop. Sonnet P2. Artifacts: `probe-phase25aq-history-seed.mjs`, `phase25aq-history-seed-report.md`.
- ‚úÖ **Phase 25AQ ‚Äî STAT-VAR EXHAUSTIVE 21/21 COMPLETE**: All 12 remaining tokens (tMinY=0x29, tMaxY=0x2A, tSigmaY=0x2B, tSigmaXY=0x2C, tr=0x2D, te=0x2E, ta=0x2F, tb=0x30, tc=0x31, td=0x32, tSSX=0x33, tSSY=0x34) PASS via Rcl_StatVar impl at 0x08019F. Slot formula `addr = 0xD0117F + (token √ó 9)` proven for full range. After Chain2, Chain1 dispatches to 0x06CF41 (graph-related code), NOT to ParseInp. kEnter=0x05 doesn't match Chain1's key-code dispatch table ‚Äî those are graph/menu keys. **Chain1/Chain2 is the graph-style dispatch path, not the ENTER‚ÜíParseInp path.** HomeHandler WAS dispatched at step 3019, cxMain changed to 0x0585E9 at step 3028. - ‚úÖ **Phase 25AL ‚Äî Compaction Trigger FULLY TRACED (KEY FINDING)**: Full call chain: 0x058423‚Üí0x05E7F7‚Üícall 0x07FF7B (pre-flush)‚Üícall 0x08384F (FindSym-related)‚Üícall 0x05E3A2 (compaction entry, step 18277)‚Üícall 0x05E836 (edit wrapper, step 18278)‚Üícall 0x0831A4 (EditProg, step 18279)‚ÜíLDDR at 0x04C990 zeros cx at step 18282. The call to 0x05E3A2 is UNCONDITIONAL ‚Äî no conditional branch guards it. Compaction is a two-phase operation: first calls EditProg (LDDR zeros cx as side effect), then optionally does a second LDDR on workspace pointers at 0xD0243A/0xD0243D. The cx-zeroing happens because workspace pointers overlap the cx range due to missing allocator/VAT initialization. Watched addresses NOT hit: 0x05E872 (buffer flush), 0x05E820 (BufToBtm), 0x0585E9 (second-pass handler), 0x0973C8 (ENTER key path). Sonnet P2. Artifacts: `probe-phase25al-compaction-trigger.mjs`, `phase25al-compaction-trigger-report.md`.

### Completed (session 93)
- ‚úÖ **Phase 25AH ‚Äî 0x04C990 = negate-BC utility, NOT cxCurApp zeroing (CORRECTS session 92)** ‚Äî Full disassembly of 0x04C950-0x04CA50 (256 bytes). 0x04C990 is a 12-byte function: `push hl; ld hl,0; or a; sbc hl,bc; push hl; pop bc; pop hl; ret`. Zero memory writes ‚Äî only stack PUSH/POP. The entire region is a library of arithmetic helpers: 0x04C950=divHL_by_10, 0x04C963=divHL_by_A_24bit, 0x04C973=cpHL_DE_preserve, 0x04C979=cpHL_DE_24bit, 0x04C980=min_HL_BC, 0x04C990=negate_BC, 0x04C99C=negate_DE, 0x04C9A8=signExtTemp_store. None reference cxCurApp (0xD007E0) or cxMain (0xD007CA). Session 92's watchpoint reporting PC=0x04C990 was misattributed ‚Äî likely post-write PC advancement where the actual zeroing instruction was 1-2 steps earlier in the caller's instruction stream. ### Completed (session 88)
- ‚úÖ **Phase 25AC ‚Äî ParseInp "variable recall" = TOKEN STREAM REDIRECT (ROOT CAUSE)** ‚Äî P1 probe dumped memory around DE before/after ParseInp with OP1=varA + stored 42.0. begPC was set to 0xD1A883 (DE+2), curPC to 0xD1A884 ‚Äî ParseInp redirected the token stream to the variable's data area, parsing BCD bytes as tokens. With overlapping 42.0 writes (probe design flaw), got errNo=0x88 and missing_block at 273 steps. BUT the key finding stands: stored 42.0 at DE was NOT overwritten by ParseInp in the clean P2 probe (variable A data survived intact at `[00 81 42 00 00 00 00 00 00]`). The "recall returns 0.0" mystery is solved: ParseInp doesn't recall ‚Äî it re-parses variable content as tokens. For Real variables (9 BCD bytes, not token data), this produces 0.0. Sonnet P1 created probe + ran. Artifacts: `probe-phase25ac-recall-offset.mjs`, `phase25ac-recall-offset-report.md`.
- ‚úÖ **Phase 25AC ‚Äî Both vars (A+Ans) confirms errNo is OP1-content-driven** ‚Äî Scenario A (both vars, OP1=varA): 720 steps, errNo=0x00, OP1=0.0 (same "found" path). Scenario B (both vars, OP1=zeros): 908 steps, errNo=0x8D, OP1=5.0 (Ans existence reduces steps by 11). Scenario C (control): 919 steps. Creating Ans does NOT clear errNo=0x8D; only having OP1 point to a valid variable name clears it. Variable "A" data (42.0) survived ParseInp in Scenario A ‚Äî confirming ParseInp doesn't modify variable data during the "found" path. Sonnet P2 created probe + ran and verified. Artifacts: `probe-phase25ac-both-vars.mjs`, `phase25ac-both-vars-report.md`.
- ‚úÖ **Phase 25AC ‚Äî StoAns STORES 5.0 when Ans exists (CONFIRMED)** ‚Äî Full PC trace comparison: Without Ans (919 steps), StoAns sets OP1[0]=0xFF at step 870 (PC=0x099A9B), ChkFindSym at step 879, FindSym at step 890, both fail ‚Üí 49-step failure path (PCs 0x099ABA/0x099ABF/0x099AC1). With Ans pre-created (903 steps), StoAns at step 875 jumps from 0x099AB3 directly to 0x099AF1 (skipping ChkFindSym entirely), OP1[0] NEVER reaches 0xFF, and FindSym success path uses PCs 0x084711/0x08471B/0x084723. **Ans data at DE=0xD1A881 contains `[00 80 50 00 00 00 00 00 00]` = 5.0 after ParseInp.** The 16-step difference is exactly the failed ChkFindSym path being eliminated. errNo=0x8D persists in both scenarios (set at step 27/32 by initial ChkFindSym on OP1=zeros). Sonnet P3 created probe + ran and verified. Artifacts: `probe-phase25ac-stoans-trace.mjs`, `phase25ac-stoans-trace-report.md`.

- ‚úÖ **Phase 25AB ‚Äî Variable recall returns 0.0, NOT 42.0 (UNEXPECTED FINDING)** ‚Äî MEM_INIT ‚Üí CreateReal("A") ‚Üí write 42.0 at DE=0xD1A881 ‚Üí set OP1=varA ‚Üí ParseInp("2+3"): 710 steps, errNo=0x00, OP1=[00 80 00 00 00 00 00 00 00]=0.0. The "found" path takes 710 steps (vs 253 with zero data in session 86, vs 918 without variable). OP1 decoded to 0.0 ‚Äî the recall mechanism works (errNo=0x00 confirms variable found) but returns wrong value. Two hypotheses: (a) allocator activity during ParseInp (newDataPtr moved 0xD1A88A‚Üí0xD1A893) overwrites the stored 42.0 at DE, or (b) the VAT data offset from DE is wrong. Control baseline matched: 918 steps, OP1=5.0, errNo=0x8D. Sonnet P2 created probe + ran and verified. Artifacts: `probe-phase25ab-parseinp-recall.mjs`, `phase25ab-parseinp-recall-report.md`.
- ‚úÖ **Phase 25AB ‚Äî 0x03E1B4 = flash unlock wrapper (CORRECTS session 86)** ‚Äî Full static disassembly of 0x03E180..0x03E200. 0x03E1B4 entry: `LD (0xD00542),A` (save A to scratch), `LD A,I` √ó 2 (eZ80 bug workaround to read interrupt state), DI, PUSH AF, restore A from scratch, `CALL 0x03E187` (flash unlock), save A to scratch, POP AF, conditional EI based on saved interrupt state, restore A, RET. 0x03E187: NOP√ó4, PUSH AF, XOR A, DI, `JR +0`, DI, RSMIX, `IM ADL`, `OUT0 (0x28),A` (flash unlock), `IN0 A,(0x28)`, `BIT 2,A`, `IN0 A,(0x06)`, `RES 2,A`, `OUT0 (0x06),A` (disable flash protection), `LD A,0x88`, `OUT0 (0x24),A` (flash command), `CP 0x88` (anti-tamper), `JP NZ,0x000066` (reset if tampered), POP AF, RET. **Session 86's claim that 0x03E1B4 "persists errNo" was WRONG** ‚Äî errNo is written at 0x061DB2 directly. 0x03E1B4 unlocks flash protection state, likely so the OS can read error strings from flash ROM. Sonnet P3 created probe + ran and verified. Artifacts: `probe-phase25ab-error-routine-disasm.mjs`, `phase25ab-error-routine-disasm-report.md`.

- ‚úÖ **Phase 25Z ‚Äî PopErrorHandler seed ADDED (0x061DD1)** ‚Äî Only this address was missing from transpiled blocks; 0x061DB2 (JError), 0x061DEF (PushErrorHandler), and 0x061E27 (normal-return stub) already existed as transpiled blocks. PopErrorHandler (0x061DD1-0x061DEE) is a 30-byte stub: `LD HL,(OPBase); POP DE (opsDelta); ADD HL,DE; LD (OPS),HL; POP DE (fpsDelta); LD HL,(FPSbase); ADD HL,DE; LD (FPS),HL; POP HL (prevErrSP); LD (errSP),HL; LD A,(errNo); RET`. Codex P1 added seeds; Opus retranspiled and verified. Artifacts: modified `scripts/transpile-ti84-rom.mjs`.
- ‚úÖ **Phase 25Z ‚Äî Full error-frame probe CHANGED BEHAVIOR** ‚Äî With PopErrorHandler now transpiled, the 25Y probe no longer fails at 37 steps with missing_block. Now runs 50K steps (max_steps), errorRestoreHits=1 (PopErrorHandler fires), but all allocator pointers zeroed and stuck at 0x006202. **ROOT CAUSE**: probe's hlPayload=0x000000 becomes PopErrorHandler's RET address ‚Üí execution jumps to 0x000000 (boot entry) ‚Üí reinitializes everything ‚Üí counting loop. The full error frame needs ParseInp's actual error continuation address as hlPayload, which is unknown. The minimal 6-byte catch frame (25X probe) works because longjmp bypasses PopErrorHandler entirely. Artifacts: probe results only (no new files).
- ‚úÖ **Phase 25Z ‚Äî CreateReal + ParseInp FULL PIPELINE (MAJOR FINDING)** ‚Äî MEM_INIT (18 steps) ‚Üí CreateReal("A") at 0x08238A (231 steps, errNo=0x00, OPBase 0xD3FFFF‚Üí0xD3FFF6 delta=-9, DE=0xD1A881 points to 9 zero bytes of new variable) ‚Üí ParseInp (253 steps, errNo=0x00). **errNo=0x8D IS FIXED by pre-creating variable "A"**. BUT OP1=[00 41 00 00 00 00 00 00 00] (unchanged from variable name setup), decoded=0, NOT 5.0. Parser with pre-created variable follows a DIFFERENT code path ‚Äî returns in 253 steps (vs 918 without variable) without computing the expression. **Hypothesis**: ParseInp's ChkFindSym at entry finds variable "A" in VAT ‚Üí parser takes "recall variable" path instead of "parse expression" path. Variable data at DE=0xD1A881 is all zeros post-ParseInp (5.0 not stored there either). Codex P3 created probe; Sonnet P3 ran and verified. Artifacts: `probe-phase25z-full-pipeline.mjs`, `phase25z-full-pipeline-report.md`.
- ‚úÖ **Phase 25Z ‚Äî Executor fallback investigation COMPLETE** ‚Äî Confirmed executor has NO raw-byte interpreter fallback (cpu-runtime.js:1064-1087). When a PC has no transpiled block, it tries skipping up to 16 bytes ahead; if no block found, terminates with 'missing_block'. ParseInp's 918-step run visits only 3 error-region PCs (0x061D3A, 0x061DB2, 0x061DBA), all transpiled blocks ‚Äî zero missing-block events. PopErrorHandler (0x061DD1) is never visited in the minimal catch frame path because longjmp does `LD SP,(errSP); POP AF; RET` directly to FAKE_RET. Normal-return cleanup stub at 0x061E27 decoded: 3√ó POP AF (discard error frame entries), EX (SP),HL + LD (errSP),HL (restore previous errSP), cleanup, RET. Codex P2 created probe+report; Sonnet P2 also created versions and ran probe. Artifacts: `probe-phase25z-executor-fallback.mjs`, `phase25z-executor-fallback-report.md`.

OP1=0, curPC unchanged. **ROOT CAUSE**: JError/PushErrorHandler addresses 0x061DB2-0x061E27 are NOT in transpiled blocks. The executor's raw-byte fallback apparently handles these blocks in the committed probe (918 steps), but direct entry via the full error frame triggers a hard missing-block stop. Adding these addresses as transpiler seeds is the fix. Codex P1 created probe; Sonnet P1 confirmed results. Entry: `XOR A; LD (0xD022BE),A` (clear flag), calls 0x099B81 twice (clears 12 IY flag bits: IY+6,7=0, res bits in IY+20,26,31,32,48,49,62,72,73,88). Then `CALL 0x099B18` which calls ChkFindSym, and if found: walks VAT entry (skip 9 bytes + var size + 1), stores to asm_data_ptr2 (0xD00687), calls helpers, WRITES begPC and curPC: `LD (0xD02317),HL; LD (0xD0231A),HL`. **ParseInp writes curPC from VAT data, does NOT read caller-seeded value.** Token reading confirmed deeper at 0x09BAB8: `LD BC,(curPC); LD HL,(endPC); SBC HL,BC; LD A,(HL)` ‚Äî reads byte at curPC, checks bounds. OPS (0xD02593) is read by helper 0x09BEED after allocation via 0x082BB5 ‚Äî it's a downward-growing OPS stack for parser operands, NOT a token reader. Codex P2 + Sonnet P2 both produced results. Artifacts: `probe-phase25y-parseinp-entry-disasm.mjs`, `phase25y-parseinp-entry-disasm-report.md`.

Only reached in pre-OPS-fix probes where corrupted error recovery left HL‚âÝDE. Current probe never visits this address. Codex P3 + Sonnet P3 confirmed. - ‚úÖ **Phase 25V ‚Äî VAT/heap initializer FOUND at 0x09DEE9 (KEY DISCOVERY)** ‚Äî Static ROM scan found ALL references to OPBase/OPS/pTemp/progPtr/FPSbase/FPS. **243 total refs, 56 writes, 11 clusters**. The REAL initializer is **Cluster 11 at 0x09DEE9..0x09DF05**: 6 consecutive `LD (nn), HL` stores writing FPSbase‚ÜíFPS‚Üí(newDataPtr 0xD025A0)‚ÜípTemp‚ÜíOPBase‚ÜíOPS‚ÜíprogPtr. The routine at 0x09DEF5 loads `LD HL, 0xD3FFFF` (symTable end) before writing pTemp/OPBase/OPS/progPtr. **Initial values are 0xD3FFFF (symTable), NOT 0xD1A881 (userMem)** ‚Äî this explains why our probes with OPBase=userMem hit ErrMemory. Other notable clusters: 0x0820FA (4 ptrs, likely allocator cleanup), 0x083675 (4 ptrs, likely memory compaction), 0x09DCAF (2 ptrs, secondary init). Codex created probe; Opus ran and verified. Artifacts: `probe-phase25v-vat-init-search.mjs`, `phase25v-vat-init-search-report.md`.
- ‚úÖ **Phase 25V ‚Äî Pointer slot naming (1/4 named, 3 genuinely unnamed)** ‚Äî 0xD02567 = `fmtMatSym` (confirmed from ti84pceg.inc). 0xD01FEA/0xD01FF0/0xD01FF6 NOT in ti84pceg.inc ‚Äî fall in undocumented gap between DeltaY(0xD01FB7) and TraceStep(0xD0203D). 6-byte stride. ROM refs concentrated in graph/finance code: 0x04xxxx (finance routines), 0x0Axxxx (graph renderer), 0x06xxxx (graphing engine), 0x0Bxxxx (program editor). All 3 are loaded as addresses into HL/DE for InsertMem adjustment ‚Äî they're pointers INTO graph/finance data, not the data itself. Codex created probe; Opus ran and verified. Artifacts: `probe-phase25v-pointer-slots.mjs`, `phase25v-pointer-slots-named-report.md`.

(2) 0x082823 = per-pointer adjuster: reads 3-byte ptr from (HL), compares against DE via SBC. `ret nc` skips if ptr >= DE. On carry path: loads delta from signExtTemp into BC, loads ptr into IX, adds delta, writes back. (3) 0x0827CA = calling loop: stores BC directly to signExtTemp, then iterates over **11 system pointer slots** (pTemp, progPtr, editSym, tSymPtr1/2, chkDelPtr3/4, plus 4 newly-discovered slots: 0xD01FEA, 0xD01FF0, 0xD01FF6, 0xD02567) calling adjustOnePtr for each. Pipeline: `InsertMem(BC)‚Üínegate(BC)‚Üístore(signExtTemp)‚Üíadjust(11 slots)`. Codex succeeded on first attempt + Sonnet verified. Artifacts: `probe-phase25u-signexttemp.mjs`, `phase25u-signexttemp-report.md`.

Computes BC = -BC. Does NOT read or write any RAM pointers. Session 78's hypothesis that 0x04C990 adjusts OPBase/pTemp/progPtr was WRONG ‚Äî it just prepares the negative delta for the actual pointer adjusters. Codex succeeded on first attempt. Artifacts: `probe-phase25t-ptr-adjuster.mjs`, `phase25t-ptr-adjuster-report.md`.
- ‚úÖ **Phase 25T ‚Äî InsertMem pointer-update subs FULLY MAPPED** ‚Äî All 4 InsertMem sub-calls disassembled + their call targets: (1) **0x082739** = VAT pointer walker: walks backward from 0xD3FFFF to OPBase, adjusting VAT entry data pointers in the moved range. Reads OPBase as loop bound only. (2) **0x0824D6** = edit-buffer adjuster: adjusts editCursor/editTail/editBtm at 0xD02317/1A/1D. (3) **0x0824FD** = bulk pointer updater: adjusts 12 pointer slots via 0x0825D1 primitive (0xD0066F-D00684, D0069F, D006A2, D0256A, D025A0). (4) **0x082823** = actual per-pointer adjuster: reads signExtTemp from 0xD02AD7, applies `if ptr >= DE: ptr += signExtTemp`. Called from 0x0827CA for pTemp, progPtr, and 5 other system pointers (0xD0244E, 0xD0257B-0xD02584). **KEY FINDING: OPBase (0xD02590) is NEVER WRITTEN by any InsertMem sub**. The corruption 0xD1A881‚Üí0xA88100 is from LDIR/LDDR block move physically overwriting OPBase's storage location because fake seed values put OPBase in the moved range. Codex P4 failed; Sonnet P2 and P4 both succeeded with comprehensive coverage. Artifacts: `probe-phase25t-insertmem-subs.mjs`, `phase25t-insertmem-subs-report.md`, `phase25t-ptr-adjuster-report.md`.

Longjmp at 0x061DB2 does `ld sp,(errSP); pop af; ret` ‚Üí landing at PopErrorHandler 0x061DD1 which restores OPS/FPS/errSP. **ParseInp called with seeded errSP + FPSbase(0xD0258A)/FPS(0xD0258D) ‚Üí RETURNS TO FAKE_RET after 85,312 steps.** errNo=0x8E (ErrMemory). Parser internally catches ErrUndefined at 0x061D3A ‚Üí JError ‚Üí recovery at 0x099929 ‚Üí cleanup at 0x082266 ‚Üí ErrMemory at 0x061D3E ‚Üí JError ‚Üí returns to FAKE_RET. OP1 unchanged ([00 41 00 00 00 00 00 00 00]). **First successful ParseInp return in project history.** Critical missing piece was FPSbase/FPS seeding ‚Äî without valid FPS pointers the longjmp cleanup crashed. - ‚úÖ **Phase 25S ‚Äî 0x082BBE region mapped** ‚Äî Not a single subroutine but ~15 small utility functions: stream byte reader (reads from pointer at 0xD025A3, auto-advances), HL+6/HL-7 helpers for VAT entry navigation, 3-byte pointer read/write primitives, type classifier (AND 0x3F + table lookup), FindSym wrappers with 3 error-handling flavors (find-or-error, find-or-error+flag-reset, error-if-found for duplicate-create prevention). - ‚úÖ **Phase 25S ‚Äî errNo=0x88 = E_Syntax RESOLVED** ‚Äî Error 0x88 = `8 + E_EDIT` (0x80) = Syntax Error with "allow re-edit" flag. 7 write sites to errNo in ROM: canonical ThrowError at 0x061DB2 plus save/clear/restore patterns in parser (e.g. 0x08515E-0x08516D saves errNo, clears it, calls variable lookup, unconditionally restores). VAT loop at 0x084711 is linear backward search comparing 3-byte name keys from OP1+1 (0xD005F9-FB). **Hypothesis confirmed**: longjmp fires but is caught by PushErrorHandler frame set up before ParseInp. errNo=0x88 persists as latent RAM state ‚Äî normal TI-OS behavior, not a transpiler bug. - ‚úÖ **Phase 25S ‚Äî Type guard 0x080084 DISASSEMBLED** ‚Äî Three entry points: (1) 0x080084: tests raw A against 0x15 (equation), 0x17 (complex), falls through to 0x05 (real), 0x16 (new equation), 0x06 (list). (2) 0x08008C: loads A from OP1[0] via GetTypeFromOP1 (0x07F7BD = `LD A,(0xD005F8); AND 0x3F; RET`) then falls into same test chain. (3) 0x0800A0: CheckSplitFlag entry (IY+0x14 bit 3). Accepted type codes: **0x05** (real), **0x06** (list), **0x15** (equation), **0x16** (new equation), **0x17** (complex). Name-length helper 0x0820CD: CPIR scan of OP1[1..8] for null terminator, returns length in A (1-8). List vars (OP1[1]=0x5D) get length bumped to 2. A‚â•7 rejection by caller. Sonnet fallback. Artifacts: `probe-phase25s-typeguard-disasm.mjs`, `phase25s-typeguard-disasm-report.md`.

- ‚úÖ **Phase 25R ‚Äî Create allocator 0x0822D9 FULLY MAPPED** ‚Äî Static disassembly of the shared Create allocator that CreateReal/CreateCplx/all CreateXxx variants jump to. **Full control flow**: (1) stores type byte A‚ÜíOP1[0] at 0x0822D9, (2) calls 0x080084 type guard (Z flag determines path), (3) reads OP1+1 for name prefix ‚Äî `]` (0x5D, list) takes special path via 0x0820CD (name-length helper) with A‚â•7 rejection‚Üí0x061D1A error, all other prefixes branch to 0x08234A alternate path, (4) saves computed A, calls 0x082BBE (pointer/slot helper, preserves HL‚ÜíBC=size), (5) calls 0x0821B9 (heap/VAT move), (6) snapshots result pointer DE‚ÜíOP1+3, clears OP1+2, restores count‚ÜíOP1+6, computes BC=count+7, calls 0x0820F1, reloads DE from OP1+3, returns at 0x082349. **Subroutines**: 0x080084, 0x0820CD, 0x082BBE, 0x0821B9, 0x07F8A2, 0x0820F1. **Error exits**: `jp nc, 0x061D1A` and 0x082BB9‚Üí0x061D3E. **Reads-before-write**: OP1+1(0xD005F9), OP4(0xD00619). CreateTemp helper 0x08359B also mapped: increments pTempCnt(0xD02596), writes `$`‚ÜíOP1+1, calls FindSym(0x0846EA). Artifacts: `probe-phase25r-create-allocator.mjs`, `phase25r-create-allocator-report.md`.

- ‚úÖ **Phase 25Q ‚Äî Error handler 0x061DB2 disassembly ‚Äî RESOLVED (LONGJMP)** ‚Äî Static disassembly of the TI-OS error convergence point. **0x061DB2 is a classic setjmp/longjmp**: (1) `ld (errNo=0xD008DF), a` stores error code, (2) `call 0x03E1B4` interrupt-safe cleanup wrapper (saves A to scratch 0xD00542, checks `ld a,i / jp pe`, DI, calls 0x03E187, restores EI state), (3) clears 4 IY-offset flag bits (IY+75 bit7, IY+18 bit2, IY+36 bit4, IY+73 bit1), (4) **`ld sp, (errSP=0xD008E0)` ‚Äî THE LONGJMP**, (5) `pop af; ret` ‚Äî returns to whatever address was saved at the errSP frame. **Does NOT call DispErrorScreen (0x062160)**. The 0x58c35b "crash" is caused by uninitialized errSP (0xFF fill) ‚Üí garbage SP ‚Üí garbage return address. DispErrorScreen is called by the recovery point (the "setjmp" side), not by the error handler itself. Gap region 0x061D80-0x061DB1 confirmed as tail of error dispatch table (13 more entries with error codes 0x28, 0x2E, 0xAB, 0xAC, 0xAF, 0x2F, 0x30, 0x31, 0xB4, 0x9F, 0xB5, 0x36). CreateReal at 0x08238A sets A=0(RealObj), HL=9(size), then `jr 0x082386 ‚Üí jp 0x0822D9`. (2) CreateCplx at 0x082380 sets A=0x0C, HL=18(=2√ó9). Those values are list/string/program/complex NAME PREFIX bytes, not type codes. (4) **0xD00619 = OP4** (confirmed from ti84pceg.inc). Bit 3 of OP4 tested post-allocation to tag complex entries with 0x0C. (5) **ADDRESS CORRECTIONS**: progPtr=0xD0259D (not 0xD01C00 as previously guessed), pTemp=0xD0259A, OPBase=0xD02590, pTempCnt=0xD02596, symTable=0xD3FFFF. - ‚úÖ **Phase 25P ‚Äî VAT disassembly (KEY DISCOVERY)** ‚Äî Static disassembly of CreateReal entry 0x08238A and crash paths 0x061D1A/0x061D3E/0x03E1B4/0x03E1CA. **0x061D1A-0x061D7E is the TI-OS error code dispatch table**, NOT stack corruption. Every entry: `ld a, <error_code>; jr 0x061db2`. CreateReal at 0x08239c does `ld a, (0xD005F9)` (OP1+1 = type byte), compares against 0x5D (list), 0x24, 0x3A, 0x72 ‚Äî if none match ‚Üí `jp nz, 0x061d46` ‚Üí error 0x8F. Our session-73 probe set OP1[1]=0x41 (name "A") when the code expects a TYPE byte at that position. CreateReal also reads 0xD00619 after the type check (bit 3 test). The 0x03E1B4 subroutine is an interrupt-safe scratch routine using 0xD00542 as temporary. IY+18 (0xD00092) is touched by `set 2, (iy+18)`. No IX-offset reads found in any disassembled range. Sonnet fallback used (Codex timed out). Artifacts: `probe-phase25p-vat-disasm.mjs`, report.
- Golden regression 26/26 PASS post-session. 3 Codex + 1 Sonnet fallback dispatches.

### Completed (session 74)
- ‚úÖ **Phase 25O ‚Äî FP primitives (FPMult, FPDiv, TenX) ‚Äî all 3 PASS** ‚Äî FPMult(6√ó7)=42.0 exact (OP1 `00 81 42 00 00 00 00 00 00`), FPDiv(84/2)=42.0 exact, TenX(10^3)=1000.0 exact (OP1 `00 83 10 00 00 00 00 00 00`). All return cleanly to FAKE_RET. Entry points: FPMult=0x07C8B7, FPDiv=0x07CAB9, TenX=0x07E219. Artifacts: `probe-phase25o-{fpmult,fpdiv,tenx}.mjs`, 3 reports. Total validated FP primitives now: FPAdd, FPSub, FPMult, FPDiv, FPSquare, SqRoot, Sin, Cos, Tan, LnX, TenX, CpOP1OP2 (12 total).
- ‚úÖ **Phase 25O ‚Äî Stat-var expansion ‚Äî 4/4 PASS** ‚Äî Extended Sto/Rcl round-trip beyond tMean to 4 new tokens: tStatN(0x02)=10.0, tXMean(0x03)=25.5, tSumX(0x04)=100.0, tMinX(0x08)=-3.0. All store and recall exact, including negative value (-3.0 encoded as `80 80 30 00 00 00 00 00 00`). Slot formula `0xD0117F + (A √ó 9)` confirmed for all tokens. Total validated stat-var tokens: tMean(0x21), tStatN(0x02), tXMean(0x03), tSumX(0x04), tMinX(0x08) = 5 total. Artifacts: `probe-phase25o-statvar-expansion.mjs`, report.
- ‚úÖ **Phase 25O ‚Äî ParseInp helper disassembly ‚Äî KEY FINDING** ‚Äî Static disassembly of the three helper subroutines ParseInp calls early: (1) `0x099B81` is pure IY-offset flag manipulation (resets parser state bits at IY+6, IY+7, IY+62, IY+32, IY+88, IY+26, IY+31, IY+73, IY+72) ‚Äî no pointer reads. (2) `0x099B18` calls ChkFindSym(0x08383D), stores DE into asm_ram(0xD00687) as scratch, then WRITES begPC(0xD02317) and curPC(0xD0231A) ‚Äî these are outputs, not inputs, explaining why seeding them in session 73 had no effect. (3) `0x09BEED` reads `OPS (0xD02593)` ‚Äî this is the critical input pointer. Loop at 0x084711 reads OP1+1(0xD005F9) as a byte compare, not a pointer fetch. **Conclusion**: next ParseInp probe should seed OPS=0xD02593. Artifacts: `probe-phase25o-parseinp-helpers.mjs`, report.
- Golden regression 26/26 PASS post-session. All 3 Codex dispatches succeeded on first attempt.

### Completed (session 73)
- ‚úÖ **Phase 25L ‚Äî FP edge pack (FPSub, FPSquare, CpOP1OP2)** ‚Äî Three probes mirroring 25I-fpadd template. **FPSub(5-3)=2.0** exact (OP1 `00 80 20 00 00 00 00 00 00`), **FPSquare(7¬≤)=49.0** exact (OP1 `00 81 49 00 00 00 00 00 00`), **CpOP1OP2** 3-case probe confirms standard TI flag convention: lt (3<5) ‚Üí F=0xA3 (C=1 Z=0), eq (5=5) ‚Üí F=0x42 (C=0 Z=1), gt (7>2) ‚Üí F=0x02 (C=0 Z=0). All three cases produce distinct flag states. Artifacts: `probe-phase25l-{fpsub,fpsquare,cpop1op2}.mjs`, 3 reports. All 3 PASS.
- ‚úÖ **Phase 25M ‚Äî Sto_StatVar round-trip** ‚Äî Follow-up to Phase 25J positive-path Rcl. Seeded OP1=42.0, A=tMean=0x21, statsValid bit 6 set, called Sto_StatVar impl 0x09A3BD. Slot at 0xD012A8 transitioned from `ff √ó 9` ‚Üí `00 81 42 00 00 00 00 00 00` = 42.0 exact. Round-trip via Rcl_StatVar with OP1 cleared to 0xFF returned 42.0 exact (diff=0). First validated STORE direction for stat vars ‚Äî establishes the full read/write pattern for all stat variables. Artifacts: `probe-phase25m-sto-statvar.mjs`, `phase25m-sto-statvar-report.md`. PASS.
- ‚ùå **Phase 25K ‚Äî ParseInp (informative FAIL)** ‚Äî Called 0x099914 with tokenized `2+3` bytes `0x32 0x70 0x33 0x3F` at userMem=0xD1A881, seeded 8 parser-pointer globals to userMem, primed HL. Probe ran to max_steps=200000 looping at 0x082be2/0x084711/0x084716/0x08471b without returning. **Key finding**: first 32 ROM bytes show `xor a; ld (0xD022BE),a; call 0x099B81; ...` ‚Äî ParseInp is pointer-driven via a global slot we haven't identified. The 8 pointer slots we seeded were all ignored. Real contract lives in the helpers at 0x099B81/0x099B18/0x09BEED which need disassembly. OP1 untouched. Artifacts: `probe-phase25k-parseinp.mjs`, `phase25k-parseinp-report.md`. Valuable negative result for next-session research.
- ‚ùå **Phase 25N ‚Äî ChkFindSym (informative FAIL)** ‚Äî CreateReal with OP1=[00 41 00 00 00 00 00 00 00] ("A" real var) jumped to 0x58c35b after 50 steps (term=missing_block). ChkFindSym jumped to 0x7eedf3 after 9 steps. The 0x58c35b address is the **known stack-corruption pattern** from CLAUDE.md home-stage-1/4 crash notes. VAT routines need stack/IX setup our postInitState doesn't provide ‚Äî possibly seeding VAT head pointers (progPtr/pTemp) or correcting IX. Recent PCs captured: 0x082bba ‚Üí 0x061d3e ‚Üí 0x061db2 ‚Üí 0x03e1b4 ... 0x082bc2 ‚Üí 0x03e1ca ‚Üí 0x061dba ‚Üí 0x58c35b. Artifacts: `probe-phase25n-chkfindsym.mjs`, `phase25n-chkfindsym-report.md`. Research needed before retry.
- Golden regression 26/26 PASS post-session. 3 parallel Codex dispatches succeeded (25L, 25M) + 2 timed out but wrote usable FAIL probes (25K, 25N).

### Completed (session 72)
- ‚úÖ **fp-real.mjs hardened** ‚Äî Carry-overflow normalization: if `toPrecision(14)` rounding pushes a digit ‚â•10, propagate carry; if MSB overflows, shift right and increment exponent. NaN/Inf now throws `Error('fp-real: cannot encode ...')` instead of silently mapping to zero. Self-test extended from 7‚Üí14 cases including carry boundary (9.999...‚Üí10.0), max 14-digit integer, tiny exponent (1e-99), negative small, œÄ, plus NaN/Inf throw assertions. All 14 PASS.
- ‚úÖ **Phase 25J ‚Äî Extended FP probes (Cos, Tan, LnX)** ‚Äî Three new probes following the Phase 25I template. **Cos(œÄ/3)=0.5** exact (OP1 `00 7F 50 00 00 00 00 00 00`). **Tan(œÄ/4)=0.9999999999999** (OP1 `00 7F 99 99 99 99 99 99 99`, diff ~1e-14 ‚Äî the TI FP engine computes correctly to 14-digit BCD precision but doesn't round to exact 1.0). **LnX(e)=0.99999999999995** (OP1 `00 7F 99 99 99 99 99 99 95`, diff ~5e-14). All 3 PASS. **Key observation**: Tan and LnX demonstrate the precision ceiling of the TI 14-digit BCD engine ‚Äî results are correct to the last representable digit but don't employ guard-digit rounding to snap to "nice" values. This is consistent with documented TI calculator behavior.
- ‚úÖ **Phase 25J ‚Äî Positive-path Rcl_StatVar** ‚Äî Follow-up to 25H-b. Seeded 42.0 at tMean stat-var slot 0xD012A8 (address derived from statVars base + 9√óindex, where index comes from token‚Üíindex subroutine at 0x09A3A5 with A=tMean=0x21). Set statsValid (bit 6 of 0xD00089). Called Rcl_StatVar impl 0x08019F ‚Üí OP1 = `00 81 42 00 00 00 00 00 00` = 42.0 exact. **First positive-path stat-var probe** ‚Äî confirms the full Rcl_StatVar read pipeline works end-to-end when data is present.
- ‚úÖ **Backfill JT labels** ‚Äî Created `backfill-jt-labels.mjs` that reads `phase25h-a-jump-table.json` and annotates bare hex addresses in phase reports with canonical JT names. Result: 141 files scanned, 81 modified, 2913 addresses annotated with ` (= Name)` suffixes. Massively improves readability of historical phase reports.
- All 4 tasks dispatched to Codex in parallel, all 4 succeeded on first attempt. Golden regression 26/26 PASS.

### Completed (session 71)
- ‚úÖ **Phase 25I** ‚Äî First validated FP engine probes. Built `fp-real.mjs` BCD helper (writeReal / readReal, 9-byte TI format: sign + biased exp + 7 mantissa bytes holding 14 BCD digits). Three probes against cold-boot OS, each asserting BOTH `returnHit` AND numeric tolerance: FPAdd(2+3)=5 exact, SqRoot(4)=2 exact, Sin(œÄ/6)=0.5 exact. **Surprising finding**: cold-boot + CoorMon(0x08C331) + postInitState is sufficient for the entire FP engine ‚Äî no angle-mode flag, no FPS init, no scratch-register seeding. Opposite of Phase 25H-b (unguarded primitive at JT slot) ‚Äî here the JT slots dispatch into richer engines that init their own state. **Codex review via cross-agent/v1** caught two real bugs we fixed: (a) initial Sin probe used sin(0)=0, a degenerate false-positive trap ‚Äî swapped for sin(œÄ/6)=0.5 which actually exercises the transcendental engine; (b) `cpu.push(FAKE_RET)` was relying on `cpu.madl=1` leaking from prior `runFrom('adl')` ‚Äî now forced explicitly. Both were latent pitfalls for any future probe. Known follow-ups (DONE in session 72): BCD carry-overflow normalization, NaN/Inf handling. Artifacts: `fp-real.mjs`, `probe-phase25i-{fpadd,sqroot,sin}.mjs`, `phase25i-{fpadd,sqroot,sin}-report.md`. Golden regression 26/26 PASS.

### Completed (session 70)
- ‚úÖ **Phase 25H-b** ‚Äî First subsystem-targeted probe. Called `Rcl_StatVar` JT slot 0x0204F0 ‚Üí impl 0x08019F with A=tMean=0x21 against fresh OS (statsValid clear). Result: JT slot returns cleanly with OP1 populated (0xFFx9 from uninit stat-var table), no error banner, no carry. **Key insight (SURPRISE)**: The JT slot is a 3-instruction primitive (token‚Üíindex, index‚ÜíOP1, ret) with no statsValid guard. The classic 83+ "refuse if stats not computed" contract is enforced at a higher abstraction layer (parser / token dispatch), not at the JT slot. Probe setup verified trustworthy by Sonnet review (all 5 check points PASS: tMean=0x21, statFlags@0xD00089, statsValid=bit 6, IY=0xD00080, entry disassembly confirms no guard). Codex dispatch failed (UTF-8 encoding error in runner) ‚Äî Sonnet fallback per workflow. Artifacts: `probe-phase25h-b-rcl-statvar.mjs`, `phase25h-b-report.md`. Follow-up: for positive-path verification, either seed stat-var table + statsValid bit then re-call slot, OR call through `ParseInp` (0x099914) to exercise the full guard‚Üídispatch path.

Walked 980 entries at ROM 0x020104 (4-byte `C3 xx yy zz` JP format, 100% JP coverage) and cross-referenced against CE-Programming/toolchain `src/include/ti84pceg.inc`. 957/980 (97.7%) slots named. Key canonical entries now known: see `## Canonical OS Entry Points (JT)` below. Confirmed 3 prior probe-guessed addresses (0x062160=DispErrorScreen, 0x08C331=CoorMon, 0x0A349A=RunIndicOff ‚Äî the last being a correction from our earlier "status bar updater" label). ### Completed (session 68)
- ‚úÖ **Phase 25G-h** ‚Äî Cross-referenced scancode table outputs against authoritative TI-OS `k*` keypress equates from `ti84pceg.inc` (CE-Programming/toolchain master). **Key correction**: the table emits `_GetKey` (`k*`) codes, NOT `_GetCSC` (`sk*`) codes. Session-67 DICT labels were wrong guesses (0x09‚ÜíENTER was actually kClear; 0x80‚ÜíPI was actually kAdd; 0x82‚ÜíSIN was actually kMul; 0x84‚ÜíTAN was actually kExpon; etc.). Rewrote DICT with authoritative k* names for 0x00-0xFB (14 overwrites + 78 new). Undecoded cells: 114 ‚Üí 10 (all in NONE plane, hitting documented k* gap at 0x8E-0x97 and specifically 0x94-0x97 which the agent flagged as genuinely absent from the keypress equates block). Artifacts: `phase25g-h-report.md` (scheme source + full 0x00-0xFF derivation + conflict table), edited `phase25g-f-decode.mjs`, regenerated `phase25g-f-scancode-decoded.md`. ### Completed (session 67)
- ‚úÖ **Phase 25G-g** ‚Äî Brute-scanned all 64 keyboard-matrix cells through scanner at 0x0159C0. 63 non-zero unique _GetCSC codes + 1 documented DOWN/no-key collision at 0x00. **Key finding**: scanner returns raw MMIO scancode `((7-sdkGroup)<<4)|bit`, NOT a compact sequential form ‚Äî the "sequential" impression came from the downstream table lookup at 0x02FF0B (per 25G-d). 15 scancodes unlabeled (genuinely unused matrix cells incl. group 7 which only has ON at bit 7). Required `cpu._iy = 0xE00800` before each iteration (scanner reads MMIO via IY-offset). Artifacts: `probe-phase25g-g-getcsc-map.mjs`, `phase25g-g-map.json`, `phase25g-g-report.md`. Golden regression 26/26 PASS.
- ‚úÖ **Phase 25G-f** ‚Äî Merged session 64's raw table + 25G-d formula + 25G-g probe-verified labels + 25G-c dictionary into a unified decode. 57 rows √ó 4 planes (NONE/2nd/ALPHA/2nd+ALPHA), plane stride 57 bytes, 8 raws 0x70‚Äì0x77 correctly out-of-range (group 7 has no translation entry). 114/228 cells remain `tok:0x94..0xFF` pending TI-OS token cross-ref (Phase 25G-h). 0 label disagreements between session 64 and 25G-g sources. Artifacts: `phase25g-f-decode.mjs`, `phase25g-f-decode.out`, `phase25g-f-decode.err`, `phase25g-f-scancode-decoded.md`.

### Completed (session 66)
- ‚úÖ **Phase 25G-d** ‚Äî Table index formula RESOLVED via dynamic instrumentation. Probe `probe-phase25g-d-index.mjs` (Codex two-stage: ISR + lookup entry at 0x02FF0B) captured 4 table reads at offset 0x1A for raw scancode 0x31. **Index formula: `offset = ((raw >> 4) * 8) + (raw & 0x0F) + 1`**. For raw 0x31: `(3*8)+1+1 = 26 = 0x1A`. Table byte at 0x09F7B5 = 0x90. ISR stage: zero table reads (translation happens in main-loop GetCSC path). Callers: 0x0302EB, 0x02FFAE, 0x02FFBF, 0x02FFDE. Report: `phase25g-d-report.md`. Golden regression 26/26 PASS.
- ‚úÖ **Phase 25G-e** ‚Äî Dispatch to 0x00B608 analysis COMPLETE. Probe `probe-phase25g-e-dispatch.mjs` dumped rst 0x28 handler (FP EXIT: 0x28‚Üí0x2B‚Üí0x02011C‚Üí0x04AB69‚Üí0x03AC‚Üí0x19B5‚ÜíHALT), searched all blocks for 0xAD‚Äì0xB6 range references (2019 internal, 5 external callers at 0x00156x/0x00161D‚Üí0x00B69E), and tested dynamic execution from 0x00ADB9 (41 steps, exited via rst 0x28 without reaching 0x00B608). Conclusion: 0x00B608 is deep in the FP engine's compare-and-branch dispatch, reachable only with specific FP operands. No indirect jumps ‚Äî all dispatch is direct. Report: `phase25g-e-report.md`. Golden regression 26/26 PASS.

### Completed (session 65)
- ‚úÖ **Phase 25G-b** ‚Äî Two-phase ISR event-loop probe (`probe-phase25g-eventloop.mjs`) reworked with keyboard cycle ‚Üí state reset ‚Üí no-keyboard cycle. Phase B trace confirms the event loop at 0x19BE never branches to 0x00B608; it executes 0x19BE‚Üí0x19EF‚Üí0x1A17‚Üí0x1A23‚Üí0x1A2D‚Üí0x1A32‚Üí0x19B6 HALT. Two new blocks visited (0x1A23, 0x1A2D). Reset strategy works cleanly. Report: `phase25g-b-report.md`. Golden regression 26/26 PASS.
- ‚úÖ **Phase 25G-c partial** ‚Äî Created `phase25g-c-decode.mjs` + `phase25g-c-scancode-decoded.md` + `phase25g-c-decode.out`. 228 bytes at 0x09F79B decoded via inline dictionary into 4 modifier-plane tables. Byte frequency: 144 unique bytes, 0x00 √ó36 most frequent. **Caveat**: physical-label column is unreliable ‚Äî table indexing doesn't match `(group<<4)|bit` scancode convention. Follow-up in Phase 25G-d.

### Completed (session 64)

- ‚úÖ **Phase 25G partial** ‚Äî Seeded 0x00B608 in transpiler (seed count 49,972‚Üí49,973). Block exists in prelifted JSON. Event loop probe (`probe-phase25g-eventloop.mjs`) traces 17 blocks via ISR dispatch (0x038‚Üí0x6f3‚Üí0x704‚Üí0x710‚Üí0x1713‚Üí0x719‚Üí0x19BE‚Üíevent loop‚ÜíHALT). Scan code translation table dumped to `phase25g-scancode-table-report.md` (57 keys √ó 4 modifiers). **Finding**: 0x00B608 is on the non-keyboard ISR path; keyboard-handling ISR clears system flag, preventing subsequent cycles from re-entering event loop.

### ROM
- `0x0040ee` ‚Äî font table base (1bpp 10√ó14, 28 bytes/glyph, idx = char ‚àí 0x20)
- `0x005B96` ‚Äî VRAM fill primitive
- `0x0802b2` ‚Äî `SetTextFgColor` (HL‚Üí0xD02688, DE=0xFFFF‚Üí0xD0268A, sets bit 4 of 0xD000CA)
- `0x0A190F` ‚Äî glyph byte loader + color flag check (Phase 188)
- `0x0A1A3B` ‚Äî per-row color pixel subroutine (reads fg/bg from 0xD02688/0xD0268A)
- `0x0A1939`, `0x0A19D7` ‚Äî VRAM pixel writers
- `0x062160` ‚Äî generic error banner renderer (48 permutations via 0xD008DF/0xD00824)
- `0x088720` ‚Äî restore path (copies 260 bytes: 0xD02EC7 ‚Üí 0xD006C0)
- `0x08C331` ‚Äî full OS init entry (CoorMon)
- `0x08C72F` ‚Äî CoorMon dispatch sub: `LD HL,(cxMain); JP (HL)` at 0x08C745. Called from 0x08C439 (notification broadcast) and 0x08C536 (main key dispatch)
- `0x04C990` ‚Äî cxCurApp zeroing site (session 92: zeroes cxCurApp at step 18296 when cx manually seeded). Needs disassembly
- `0x058241` ‚Äî home-screen cxMain handler target (set by 0x08C8CB). Has RET NZ guards; ParseInp deeper in call chain
- `0x0019BE` ‚Äî OS event loop entry (ISR: 0x038 ‚Üí 0x719 ‚Üí here when 0xD177BA set)
- `0x0159C0` ‚Äî direct keyboard scan (scan code in B)
- `0x0a2b72` / `0x0a29ec` / `0x0a2854` / `0x0a2106` ‚Äî home stages 1/3/4/entry-line
- `0x0a349a` ‚Äî status bar updater (guard: bit6 of 0xD0009b must be clear)
- `0x0a3320` ‚Äî status indicator dots
- `0x056900` ‚Äî dispatch table populator (dynamic-only; head=0xD0231A tail=0xD0231D)
- `0x09DEE0` ‚Äî MEM_INIT entry: heap/VAT allocator initializer. HL=0xD1A881‚ÜítempMem/FPSbase/FPS/newDataPtr; HL=0xD3FFFF‚ÜípTemp/OPBase/OPS/progPtr. Then calls 0x08A98F, sets IY+71 bit 7, flash-size‚Üí0xD025C5. RET at 0x09DF34. Single caller: 0x09DD62.
- `0x0820ED` ‚Äî compaction/delete helper: BC=9, subtracts from OPBase/pTemp/progPtr, LDIR block move. NOT boot-time init. Entry 0x0820F1 takes arbitrary BC.
- `0x09F79B` ‚Äî scan code translation table (228 bytes, 4 modifier √ó 57). Index: `((raw>>4)*8)+(raw&0x0F)+1`. Modifier offsets: none=0, 2nd=0x38, alpha=0x70, alpha+2nd=0xA8
- `0x02FF0B` ‚Äî GetCSC lookup entry (drives table read). Callers at 0x0302EB, 0x02FFAE, 0x02FFBF, 0x02FFDE
- `0x000028` ‚Äî rst 0x28 = FP EXIT (di; rsmix ‚Üí 0x2B ‚Üí 0x02011C ‚Üí 0x04AB69 ‚Üí 0x03AC ‚Üí 0x19B5 ‚Üí HALT)
- `0x00B2C4` ‚Äî FP engine operation selection hub
- `0x00B554` ‚Äî FP engine loop-back to 0x00AE24

### RAM
- `0xD02688` / `0xD0268A` ‚Äî fg / bg color registers
- `0xD00595` / `0xD00596` ‚Äî curRow / curCol (curRow wraps 0xFF via `inc a`, not sentinel)
- `0xD005F8` ‚Äî OP1, `0xD00603` ‚Äî OP2, `0xD0060E` ‚Äî OP3, `0xD00619` ‚Äî OP4, `0xD00624` ‚Äî OP5, `0xD0062F` ‚Äî OP6 (11 bytes apart, NOT 9)
- `0xD005A1-0xD005C5` ‚Äî per-char font record (IX walks this)
- `0xD006C0` ‚Äî display buffer (260 bytes, no natural writers ‚Äî use restore path)
- `0xD0058E` ‚Äî keyboard OS scan-code output
- `0xD0009B` ‚Äî system flags (bit6 = status-bar update guard)
- `0xD000c6` ‚Äî icon type selector (bit2: 0=battery, 1=mode dots)
- `0xD02EC7` ‚Äî backup buffer (seed for restore path)
- `0xD020A6` ‚Äî 26-byte mode text buffer ("Normal Float Radian       ")
- `0xD008DF` ‚Äî errNo (error code register ‚Äî written by error handler at 0x061DB2)
- `0xD008E0` ‚Äî errSP (saved SP for error longjmp ‚Äî MUST seed for CreateReal/ParseInp)
- `0xD008E3` ‚Äî errOffset
- `0xD007FA` ‚Äî onSP (ON-key handler SP)
- `0xD00542` ‚Äî scratch RAM (used by interrupt-safe wrapper at 0x03E1B4)
- `0xD00619` ‚Äî OP4 (type byte bit 3 tested by CreateReal post-allocation)
- `0xD02587` ‚Äî tempMem (initialized to userMem=0xD1A881 by MEM_INIT)
- `0xD02590` ‚Äî OPBase (VAT base pointer)
- `0xD02593` ‚Äî OPS (parser expression stack pointer ‚Äî critical input for ParseInp)
- `0xD02596` ‚Äî pTempCnt
- `0xD0259A` ‚Äî pTemp (VAT temporary pointer)
- `0xD0259D` ‚Äî progPtr (VAT program pointer ‚Äî NOT 0xD01C00 as previously guessed)
- `0xD3FFFF` ‚Äî symTable (end of VAT symbol table)
- `0xD02577` ‚Äî InsertMem scratch slot (saved BC for VAT walker)
- `0xD02AD7` ‚Äî signExtTemp (negated insertion delta, used by pointer adjuster 0x082823)
- `0xD02AD9` ‚Äî signExtFlag (high byte of signExtTemp, used by 0x04C9A8 for 24-bit right shift)
- `0xD0066F-0xD0067B` ‚Äî iMathPtr1-5 (3-byte pointer slots, adjusted by InsertMem bulk updater 0x0824FD)
- `0xD0067E/0xD00681` ‚Äî asm_data_ptr1/2 (also adjusted by InsertMem)
- `0xD0244E` ‚Äî editSym (pointer to VAT of variable being edited, adjusted by 0x082823)
- `0xD0257B/0xD0257E` ‚Äî tSymPtr1/tSymPtr2 (temp-symbol pointers, adjusted by 0x082823)
- `0xD02581/0xD02584` ‚Äî chkDelPtr3/chkDelPtr4 (delete-check pointers, adjusted by 0x082823)
- `0xD0256A` ‚Äî fmtMatMem (matrix-formatting scratch pointer, adjusted by InsertMem)
- `0xD025A0` ‚Äî newDataPtr (points into moved VAT data area, adjusted by InsertMem)
- `0xD02317/0xD0231A/0xD0231D` ‚Äî begPC/curPC/endPC (NOT editCursor/editTail/editBtm ‚Äî those are at 0xD0243A/0xD0243D/0xD02440)
- `0xD01FEA/0xD01FF0/0xD01FF6` ‚Äî editor/deletion tracking pointer slots (proposed: editPtr1/2/3) adjusted by 0x0827CA. 6-byte stride, each with +3 scratch companion (0xD01FED/0xD01FF3/0xD01FF9). Seeded from chkDelPtr3, reads via CALL 0x04C973 compare helper. NOT in ti84pceg.inc.
- `0xD02567` ‚Äî fmtMatSym (pointer to matrix-formatting symbol, adjusted by 0x0827CA)
- `0xD177BA` ‚Äî post-init flag (enables 0x719 ‚Üí 0x19BE ISR path)
- `IX = 0xD1A860` ‚Äî home-screen stage entry value

### Ports
- `0x3D/0x3E` ‚Äî IRQ status/ack. `0x5000+` ‚Äî FTINTC010. `0x500A` ‚Äî keyboard IRQ ack (OUT 0x08). `0x5006` ‚Äî keyboard IRQ mask.
- `0xF80000+` ‚Äî LCD PL111 registers (ROM writes here in ADL mode: timing0 +0x00, timing1 +0x04, timing2 +0x08, upbase +0x10, lpbase +0x14, ctrl +0x18). **Now mirrored in cpu-runtime.js alongside 0xE00000** (Phase 202g). F80000 writes are logged via `cpu.getLcdF80Stats()`.
- `0xE00000+` ‚Äî LCD MMIO as intercepted by peripherals.js (upbase +0x10, ctrl +0x18). `0xE00800-0xE00920` ‚Äî keyboard MMIO. `0xE00900` ‚Äî scan result.
- `0xD40000` ‚Äî VRAM base (BGR565)

---

## Operating Mode (Parallel Codex Dispatch)

1. **Pick up state** from this file + `git log --oneline | head -10`.
2. **Dispatch 3‚Äì4 parallel Codex agents** per session via `cross-agent.py`. CC orchestrates and verifies; Codex writes files and runs probes.
3. **Keep Codex tasks ‚â§10 min each** ‚Äî 15-min timeouts kill broader tasks. Split big investigations into (a) find X / (b) use X.
4. **Sonnet fallback** via Agent tool when Codex stalls with 0-byte output.
5. **CC verifies every deliverable** (re-run `node probe-*.mjs`) before committing.
6. **Commit + push** with message `feat: auto-session N ‚Äî Phases X/Y/Z (one-line per phase)`.
7. **Update this file** before stopping. Keep only current state + next priorities fresh.
8. **At every pause** run `/context`. <70% of 1M ‚Üí proceed. ‚â•70% ‚Üí stop and hand off.

**Dispatch command**:
```bash
python "C:/Users/rober/Downloads/Projects/Agent/runner/cross-agent.py" \
  --direction cc-to-codex --task-type implement \
  --prompt "<self-contained task: exact addresses, file paths, calling conventions>" \
  --working-dir "C:/Users/rober/Downloads/Projects/school/follow-alongs" \
  --timeout 600
```

Codex has NO conversation context. Prompts must be fully self-contained.

---

## Important Constraints

- **Don't revert dirty worktree files** ‚Äî many unrelated modifications sit in the tree intentionally.
- **Stay with 1:1-ish bytecode lift** ‚Äî widen decoder, improve CFG discovery, improve instruction semantics, add runtime helpers only to support lifted blocks. Do NOT rewrite as a high-level emulator.
- **Disable timer IRQ for OS init probes**: `createPeripheralBus({ timerInterrupt: false })`. Default 200-tick IRQ hijacks init via 0x1713 ‚Üí 0x67F8 ‚Üí 0x1c33 infinite loop.
- **ROM write-protect essential**: `cpu-runtime.js` `write8/16/24` silently drop writes where `addr < 0x400000`.
- **Keyboard matrix (SDK-authoritative)**: `keyMatrix[N] = SDK Group(7-N)`. Scan code = `(idx << 4) | bit`. 63/64 active; DOWN = 0x00 collides with no-key. Full map in `TI-84_Plus_CE/keyboard-matrix.md`.
- **`mem.fill(val, start, length)` is WRONG** ‚Äî it's `(val, start, END)`. Always use `start + length`. Fixed across 47 probes in Phase 194.

---

## How To Regenerate

```bash
node scripts/transpile-ti84-rom.mjs                      # ~2s
node TI-84_Plus_CE/test-harness.mjs                      # 25-test harness
node TI-84_Plus_CE/probe-phase99d-home-verify.mjs        # golden regression
node TI-84_Plus_CE/audit-true-uncovered.mjs              # true-coverage audit
node TI-84_Plus_CE/coverage-analyzer.mjs                 # gap analysis
( cd TI-84_Plus_CE && gzip -kf -9 ROM.transpiled.js )    # regenerate .gz
```

After committing code changes, re-run `npx gitnexus analyze` (PostToolUse hook usually handles this). Add `--embeddings` if `.gitnexus/meta.json` shows `stats.embeddings > 0`.
